[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run targeting a PDF text-extraction harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magainst Apache PDFBox has timed out after roughly [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m seconds. The main thread [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains in a parser routine, repeatedly invoking the native callback `traceCmpInt` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand then Apache PDFBox methods such as `RandomAccessRead.peek`, [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BaseParser.parseCOSDictionary`, and `XrefParser.parseXref`. No crash or exception [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis reported—only a prolonged execution that exceeds the fuzzer timeout threshold.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During a fuzzing session using Jazzer and libFuzzer, the target application fails[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto complete within the allotted time. The fuzzer reports “ERROR: libFuzzer: [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeout” after ~[0m[1;36m28.4[0m[39m s of continuous execution without termination or progress.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While no memory corruption or exception is observed, the issue manifests as a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhang or denial-of-service scenario: an input causes the parser to loop or stall [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindefinitely. This is effectively a performance/Hang vulnerability where a crafted [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDF can lock up the parsing logic.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows the main thread in a RUNNABLE state at [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.runtime.TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceCmpInt`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating heavy instrumentation but not the root cause.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Immediately below the callback, the thread is in PDFBox’s [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RandomAccessRead.peek`, then descends into:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `BaseParser.parseCOSDictionary`  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `XrefParser.parseTrailer` → `XrefParser.parseXref`  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `COSParser.retrieveTrailer` → `PDFParser.initialParse` → `PDFParser.parse`  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `Loader.loadPDF` → `PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The repeated traversal of dictionary and cross-reference parsing routines [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggests the input causes pathological behavior in trailer/XRef parsing logic.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads are blocked or deadlocked; background GC, reference-handler, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand cleaner threads appear idle or waiting normally.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To get a holistic view of why the parser hangs, reviewers should examine:  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. PDFParser initialization and parsing entry points [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFParser.initialParse`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDFParser.parse`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. XrefParser logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XrefParser.parseXref`, `XrefParser.parseTrailer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling malformed or deeply nested cross-references and trailer dictionaries.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. BaseParser’s dictionary parsing routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`BaseParser.parseCOSDictionary`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits use of `RandomAccessRead.peek` to ensure buffer bounds and termination [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. RandomAccessRead implementations to verify they cannot enter an infinite-loop [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor excessive backtracking when fed adversarial data.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only as an entry point; it is not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself responsible for the hang but may reveal how inputs are delivered to the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy focusing on these components, the investigation can determine why certain inputs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlead to unbounded parsing time without addressing the root cause directly or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproposing fixes.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
